## <a id="prompt-1997578886566285600">3Då¡é€šåœºæ™¯ä¸­çš„åˆ›æ„äºŒç»´ç </a> (<a href="https://x.com/trxuanxw/status/1997578886566285567?s=20" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Terry</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-07/1997578886566285600_0.jpg" alt="3Då¡é€šåœºæ™¯ä¸­çš„åˆ›æ„äºŒç»´ç ">

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-07/1997578886566285600_1.jpg" alt="3Då¡é€šåœºæ™¯ä¸­çš„åˆ›æ„äºŒç»´ç ">

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-07/1997578886566285600_2.jpg" alt="3Då¡é€šåœºæ™¯ä¸­çš„åˆ›æ„äºŒç»´ç ">

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-07/1997578886566285600_3.jpg" alt="3Då¡é€šåœºæ™¯ä¸­çš„åˆ›æ„äºŒç»´ç ">

```
**Task:** Create an exquisite, miniature 3D cartoon-style scene representing a specific industry, featuring a seamlessly integrated QR code.

**Perspective & Style:**
Present a charming, detailed miniature 3D scene viewed from a 45Â° top-down perspective. The style should be reminiscent of high-quality Cinema 4D rendering: refined, smoothly rounded modeling, rich textures, and stylized PBR materials. Gentle, lifelike lighting with soft shadows should create a warm, playful, and comfortable ambiance. The background should be a clean, minimalist solid color to make the miniature world pop.

**Central Focus & QR Code Integration:**
At the center of the scene, place a prominent, stylized building or main structure that embodies the **[User Input: Industry Name]**.

Crucially, the user-provided **[User Input: QR Code Image]** must be creatively and seamlessly integrated into this central area. It should **NOT** look like a flat sticker or an afterthought.
*Examples of integration:* It could be fashioned as the central plaza paving stones, embedded into the facade of the main building as a glowing architectural element, designed as a futuristic rooftop garden layout, or forming a large, stylized billboard that fits the scene's aesthetic naturally. The QR code must remain scannable but look like an intrinsic, textured part of the 3D world.

**Surrounding Details:**
Complement the central structure with proportionally-sized, playful 3D elements relevant to the **[User Input: Industry Name]**. Include charming, tiny cartoon figures engaged in industry-specific activities, appropriate miniature vehicles, and floating icons or micro-scenes that illustrate the essence of that field. The scene should be bustling with cute, detailed activity.

**Text Element:**
At the top-center of the scene, prominently display the **[User Input: Industry Name]** in a large, friendly, cartoon-style font. The text should have no background and may subtly overlap with the top edge of the 3D scene to enhance integration.

**Parameters:**
```

## <a id="prompt-1997428572038844700">æ°å…‹Â·ä¿ç½—ï¼šéšå½¢é£æŠ•å·¨æ˜Ÿ</a> (<a href="https://x.com/PolymarketMoney/status/1997428572038844578" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Polymarket Money</a>)

```
Jake Paul could be one of the best performing venture investors of the last 10 years: 

> Invested in Ramp Seed round in 2019, now valued at $32B.

> Invested in Chronosphere seed round in 2019, acquired for $3.35B in November.

> Invested in Olipop $200M series B in 2022, now valued at $1.85B.

```

```
æ°å…‹Â·ä¿ç½—å¯èƒ½æ˜¯è¿‡å»åå¹´è¡¨ç°æœ€å‡ºè‰²çš„é£æŠ•æŠ•èµ„äººä¹‹ä¸€ï¼š

> 2019å¹´å‚ä¸Rampç§å­è½®èèµ„ï¼Œè¯¥å…¬å¸ç›®å‰ä¼°å€¼320äº¿ç¾å…ƒã€‚
```

## <a id="prompt-1996526274714726400">AIã§ãƒ‹ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã‚’å›³è§£ã‚«ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã«</a> (<a href="https://x.com/felo_ai/status/1996526274714726471" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Felo AI</a>)

## <a id="prompt-2005276248789131773">å……æ°”å“ç‰Œæ ‡å¿—ï¼šæŸ”è½¯å®¢å…ç„¦ç‚¹</a> (<a href="https://x.com/TechieBySA/status/2005276248789131773" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">TechieSA</a>)

